This video is so emotional for me now. Its a little odd to think of. I used to think this video was adorable, and i always felt bad for the puppy. Now i relate to her. I caught pneumonia this year because i aspirated some water. I was sick for three weeks with my local hospital's incorrect treatment. I went into hypoxic respiratory failure and had to be admitted to another hospital a couple of hours away. It felt like being trapped in my ownnlittle bubble. I wasnt allowed to get out of bed for my first four days; i was on seven oxygen treatments.  By day five i was itching so badly to get up and move around that they finally let me. From there i just started getting better and better. Sometimes, its still a little hard to breathe, but i appreciate the little things more now. Thats how i imagine this puppy feels. Everything must be such a wonder for her.

This was such a beautiful story. You guys never gave up on her because she never gave up on herself. She knew as long as you guys were fighting for her. Then she was going to fight too. This makes me look at my two fighters in my home. My Autistic son and one of our fur babies from my son's dog. She had five puppies and by the time she was pushing out her last she was so tired. Me and my husband had to help. The last one was the biggest out of the litter. Unfortunately he wasn't breathing and I had to work fast. Cleaning out his nose and air way. Still he wasn't breathing and had to start doing CPR on the tiniest thing I ever had to. Giving him breaths and putting oxygen on next to him. It seemed like forever but I got him back. Yet the whole day was touch and go. Then he stopped breathing again at night and I had to work on him again. It was so scary and my Autistic son who was 24 at the time kept talking to him. Telling him "I we wont give up on you, Don't give up on us please!" I don't know what changed but he started to breath normally again. I kept an eye on him all night. By the next day he was eating and crying and moving around. Unfortunately they think the loss of oxygen might have caused some slower mental developments and his front leg has a deformity in the bone growth. You would never know he had anything wrong with him. It took time to catch up to his brothers and sister but he is amazing. He is the biggest out of all her litters and he is just a big puppy who just loves to play with toys and loves his mom and dad and his other two siblings from two different litters. I named him Journey because he had one heck of a journey to come into this world and stay in it. We just couldn't give him up and I'm glad we kept our special big little guy ğŸ˜Š

When it reaches the bottom, the inanimate level of reality, from which everything grows, it changes it. If we ooze ill-will, it creates negative changes throughout the system, which manifest in increasingly extreme climatic and geological events. In other words, when human relationships go out of balance, everything goes out of balance. When our relations become extreme, everything becomes extreme; when we become violent, everything becomes violent. Each summer, the ramifications of the linkage between our relations and our world become more extreme, until we acknowledge that everything that exists, exists in a connected, hierarchical system and that whoever is at the top determines the state of the rest of the system. It is not as if previously, we were better people than we are today. It is simply that there were fewer people, and therefore fewer elements that exude ill will. Also, relationships between people in the past were less toxic than they are today. While there are fewer wars today than ever, the levels of suspicion and alienation between people are skyrocketing, to the point where people can no longer trust their own family members. As a result, wars between countries are rarer than ever, but divorce rates, domestic violence, and violence in the community, are at an all-time high. Even the internet, which we invented purportedly in order to connect people, is being used to abuse, deceive, and exploit people. The world-wide-web proves that everything we create, we use against others. When there is such a negative element in a system, and that element is at the top of the system, how can the entire system not go awry? Therefore, if we want the weather to cool, the sea-level to drop, and the storms to subside, we must cool the fire and calm the storms between us. This give me hope that someday humanity's better angels will win out for the soul of our species. It always comes back to dogs for me when all other hope is lost.  Today I sat with my daughter watching the NASA mission. This was the first time in our history that humans moved a heavenly body. The goal was to one day stop an asteroid collision with the Earth. I sat there waiting, wondering to myself if it wouldn't be better for the universe had we not succeeded in this technology. If humanity was doomed to continue down the path of hatred and greed, what would stop us from spreading that across the stars, taking what we want without any consideration for the people, resources, habitats, and potentially extraterrestrials exploited? Not that there is anything I can do about that, but if I was given the choice, it seems like a safer bet would be extinction given our tract record. That, vs the potential misery that we could inflict on further generations, on this planet and beyond.  But then I come across this video and am reminded there is still another side of us battling to win out. Kindness shown when it wasn't necessary or convenient, with no ulterior motive than just to help this creature have a chance to live and be loved. It's hard for some of us to belive in a higher power. Our minds just aren't made that way. It would be of great comfort to be able to have that certainty that everything will work out in the end, but it's just not something that is possible for me. I could lie and say so but any creator worthy of worship would see through that. If they exist they built me this way, with whatever capacity for faith I have.  With that said, any time I come close to the feeling some experience in the pews on Sunday, it is when contemplating our co-evolution with dogs. They seem almost divinely sent to guide us, protecting us from the ancient caves and forests from the beasts around us, all the way to the modern era and the monsters within us. If we can continue to choose love more and more instead of hate, maybe we will some day be worthy of being amongst stars, in whatever form that takes.

So precious so sweet. Just a little TLC. And then there was life... 2 years ago my neighbor walked over with a pitbull/lab. We knew our matriarch would be going soon. She was turning 17 and slowing down. My husband looked at me and said, oh no we're going to lose luna. I said I know. Every time a dog walks in another dog walks out. He said to me, remember when we lost our matriarch labrador. And you told me wait, we're going to wait, he was looking to find a new dog to fill that missing spot.  I said wait they will find us. He's like they? How does one dog find you they is like three. I said yeah they will find us...  Well they did. Three dogs. We had them going on 10 years now.. so in our neighbor walked in with this new dog. My husband knew oh no when one door opens another one closes.   We lost our matriarch seven months later. So beautiful so lovely a white eskimo. My belka Luna. My squirrel Moon.   This new pup. So precious. She inherited of course all of the toys. The only dog that would play would be my luna. The other dogs would look at the toys like, no thanks you're funny. But Luna love to play. And her new puppy did too. So precious. Her being a pit I was worried oh no she's going to chew a part and destroy all the toys but then again so does my luna. You give her a toy, even the tough toys she can destroy within less than a week. Sometimes one day. But this dog, this dog treats them as if they are her babies. She soft mouths them.  Never once has she destroyed any of the toys. As a matter of fact, the last toy my matriarch received. And slept with for the two nights before her death. That toy She carries around like her wooby... She sleeps with it every night. I have to wash it quite often. Because she carries it around in her mouth and she'll bark and she'll talk with it in her mouth and by the end of the day it is full of so much slobber. So it gets washed quite often. But I think it's so sweet no other toys she carries around like that just Luna's.   It's amazing how dogs know. Her coming in to our world being a puppy I was worried. Especially with Luna not doing so well. But she was very careful and watched over her. Always allowed her to go before her. Was very sweet when she came up to her. Instead of she new, I'm coming in and you're leaving. I miss her so much. Sometimes I see her out of the corner of my eye. As a matter of fact the other day my husband came in and said oh my gosh I just saw Luna on the porch. I said yep you're going to catch her out of the corner of your eye. She's still with us. She hasn't left her home yet. Warms my heart. I love animals so much. They bring such love to our homes. What a blessing.

That is a awesome story...thank you so much for sharing it with us! She is a beautiful lil pup & full of so much life. Its sometimes so much easier to assume that the animal isn't gonna recover so we put em down & don't really try. But u guys gave her a chance & omgoodness she made a recovery. I had a dog that got really sick at the age of 1. The vet told me that I need to put him down cause all he is doing is suffering & he isn't gonna make it anyway. But I saw a look in his eye that was telling me not to give up on him. So I talked the Vet into sending me home with the fluids & meds that he needed plus everything else I wouldn't be able to get on my own without the vets help, cause I was gonna fight for my Boy & kno1 was gonna convince me otherwise. So I gave him fluids under the skins, IV antibiotics, pain med & anything else I had to do to keep him alive. He was a sick pup thats forsure! I even slept next to him every night so I could hear his breathing...he loved it! And then after several days & me starting to question myself if I was doing the right thing. He stood up & walked to the door to go outside. I was shocked cause I was having to help him every step of the way & sometimes even massage that area so he would go. But now my Boy was walking on his own & asking to go out...WHAT!!! It was such a awesome feeling to know he was gonna b ok & I didn't give up on him. After that day he improved daily & withing a lil over a week my beautiful big puppy was fully recovered. So I get that fight & understand why some of us just can't give up on our animals. If it was cancer & a guarantee it will spread then sure help them pass on. But when there's even a lil chance of survival I just gotta try. GOD BLESS!!!

A regular vet would tell you that putting her down would be the best course of action as it would put her out of her misery. I would agree with them myself as I have seen the effects on dogs that do not get the interaction needed during development. My dog wants NOTHING to do with you unless she wants attention, if she does not, bugger off. She hates other dogs, she also hates water. (Like being in it, she will drink it no problem, even when she should not because it is a bucket that collected rain water and has become stagnant)  She loves snow, but i remember the first year with her snow terrified her, so i suited up and went outside with her to show her snow was okay. She fell in love with it, because of development she got as a puppy.   Sally, living in the bubble will have missed out on a lot of this social and behavioral development. Like the whole interaction with other dogs.  Sally however was determined to do it. She fought for her life outside the bubble. She wanted it.
Just some friendly knowledge. If you smack her butt when shes going crazy she'll stop acting so wild.. if she doesn't stop, try a light kick... if she tries to nibble or bite, just give her a nice hard smack on the nose.. If she deficates in the house, just smack her on the ass 3 times (but no more than 3) and then rub her nose in it, and say the words "DID YOU DO THAT?" then give her 1 more smack and say the words "NO!" .. Hope this helps, I've been training dogs for years..

Ok, I've seen so many contrived videos with regard to animal rescues that my BS detector goes off pretty quickly.  This is *not* one of those cases.  The feeding tube sutured to her nose, the central line in her neck and the oxygen bubble were a reality check.  The weaning from supplemental oxygen was as real as it gets.  I spent 23 years as a nurse in a Pediatric ICU and have participated in the care of babies that have gone through this.  My hat's off to you and your team that cared for and continue to care for this puppy.  The results are nothing less than astounding.  You have every right to be proud of this outcome.  Her survival is a testament to the high quality and skill of the care you gave her and the caring of you and all your team. Very good work.    This video absolutely made my day.

for the Lord will not hold him guiltless that taketh his name in vain.  8 Remember the sabbath day, to keep it holy.  9 Six days shalt thou labour, and do all thy work:  10 But the seventh day is the sabbath of the Lord thy God: in it thou shalt not do any work, thou, nor thy son, nor thy daughter, thy manservant, nor thy maidservant, nor thy cattle, nor thy stranger that is within thy gates:  11 For in six days the Lord made heaven and earth, the sea, and all that in them is, and rested the seventh day: wherefore the Lord blessed the sabbath day, and hallowed it.  12 Honour thy father and thy mother: that thy days may be long upon the land which the Lord thy God giveth thee.  13 Thou shalt not kill.  14 Thou shalt not commit adultery.  15 Thou shalt not steal.  16 Thou shalt not bear false witness against thy neighbour.  17 Thou shalt not covet thy neighbour's house, thou shalt not covet thy neighbour's wife, nor his manservant, nor his maidservant, nor his ox, nor his ass, nor any thing that is thy neighbour's.    ..,..,..,.., .......... .,........,. ,..,,,,,,,,.., ,,.........,, ....,.....
John 3:16 [16]For God so loved the world, that he gave his only begotten Son, that whosoever believeth in him should not perish, but have everlasting life.  Luke 13:3 [3]I tell you, Nay: but, except ye repent, ye shall all likewise perish.  John 14:6 [6]Jesus saith unto him, I am the way, the truth, and the life: no man cometh unto the Father, but by me.  Jeremiah 29:13 King James Version 13 And ye shall seek me, and find me, when ye shall search for me with all your heart.   John 8:31-32 King James Version 31 Then said Jesus to those Jews which believed on him, If ye continue in my word, then are ye my disciples indeed; 32 And ye shall know the truth, and the truth shall make you free.   John 8:12 [12]Then spake Jesus again unto them, saying, I am the light of the world: he that followeth me shall not walk in darkness, but shall have the light of life.   Matthew 4:17  From that time Jesus began to preach, and to say, Repent: for the kingdom of heaven is at hand.  Romans 10:9  That if thou shalt confess with thy mouth the Lord Jesus, and shalt believe in thine heart that God hath raised him from the dead, thou shalt be saved.  Romans 10:13 For whosoever shall call upon the name of the Lord shall be saved.   Luke 6:27-38 But I say unto you which hear, Love your enemies, do good to them which hate you,  6:28 Bless them that curse you, and pray for them which despitefully use you.  6:29 And unto him that smiteth thee on the one cheek offer also the other; and him that taketh away thy cloak forbid not to take thy coat also.  6:30 Give to every man that asketh of thee; and of him that taketh away thy goods ask them not again.  6:31 And as ye would that men should do to you, do ye also to them likewise.  6:32 For if ye love them which love you, what thank have ye? for sinners also love those that love them.  6:33 And if ye do good to them which do good to you, what thank have ye? for sinners also do even the same.  6:34 And if ye lend to them of whom ye hope to receive, what thank have ye? for sinners also lend to sinners, to receive as much again.  6:35 But love ye your enemies, and do good, and lend, hoping for nothing again; and your reward shall be great, and ye shall be the children of the Highest: for he is kind unto the unthankful and to the evil.  6:36 Be ye therefore merciful, as your Father also is merciful.  6:37 Judge not, and ye shall not be judged: condemn not, and ye shall not be condemned: forgive, and ye shall be forgiven:  6:38 Give, and it shall be given unto you; good measure, pressed down, and shaken together, and running over, shall men give into your bosom. For with the same measure that ye mete withal it shall be measured to you again.   Ephesians 2:8-9 For by grace are ye saved through faith; and that not of yourselves: it is the gift of God: Not of works, lest any man should boast.  2 Chronicles 7:14 If my people, which are called by my name, shall humble themselves, and pray, and seek my face, and turn from their wicked ways; then will I hear from heaven, and will forgive their sin, and will heal their land.  Matthew 5:2-12 King James Version 2 And he opened his mouth, and taught them, saying, 3 Blessed are the poor in spirit: for theirs is the kingdom of heaven. 4 Blessed are they that mourn: for they shall be comforted. 5 Blessed are the meek: for they shall inherit the earth. 6 Blessed are they which do hunger and thirst after righteousness: for they shall be filled. 7 Blessed are the merciful: for they shall obtain mercy. 8 Blessed are the pure in heart: for they shall see God. 9 Blessed are the peacemakers: for they shall be called the children of God. 10 Blessed are they which are persecuted for righteousness' sake: for theirs is the kingdom of heaven. 11 Blessed are ye, when men shall revile you, and persecute you, and shall say all manner of evil against you falsely, for my sake. 12 Rejoice, and be exceeding glad: for great is your reward in heaven: for so persecuted they the prophets which were before you.  Matthew 24:4-14  And Jesus answered and said unto them, Take heed that no man deceive you. 24:5 For many shall come in my name, saying, I am Christ; and shall deceive many. 24:6 And ye shall hear of wars and rumours of wars: see that ye be not troubled: for all these things must come to pass, but the end is not yet. 24:7 For nation shall rise against nation, and kingdom against kingdom: and there shall be famines, and pestilences, and earthquakes, in divers places. 24:8 All these are the beginning of sorrows. 24:9 Then shall they deliver you up to be afflicted, and shall kill you: and ye shall be hated of all nations for my name's sake. 24:10 And then shall many be offended, and shall betray one another, and shall hate one another. 24:11 And many false prophets shall rise, and shall deceive many. 24:12 And because iniquity shall abound, the love of many shall wax cold. 24:13 But he that shall endure unto the end, the same shall be saved. 24:14 And this gospel of the kingdom shall be preached in all the world for a witness unto all nations; and then shall the end come.   Exodus 20 King James Version 20 And God spake all these words, saying,  2 I am the Lord thy God, which have brought thee out of the land of Egypt, out of the house of bondage.  3 Thou shalt have no other gods before me.  4 Thou shalt not make unto thee any graven image, or any likeness of any thing that is in heaven above, or that is in the earth beneath, or that is in the water under the earth.  5 Thou shalt not bow down thyself to them, nor serve them: for I the Lord thy God am a jealous God, visiting the iniquity of the fathers upon the children unto the third and fourth generation of them that hate me;  6 And shewing mercy unto thousands of them that love me, and keep my commandments.  7 Thou shalt not take the name of the Lord thy God in vain;
